I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder drops additional tool calls from same delta, causing AiMessage/tool-execution mismatch
**Describe the bug**
When using `OpenAiStreamingChatModel` on the OpenAI-compatible streaming path, tool execution can diverge from the final `AiMessage`:

- all tool calls are emitted and processed via `onCompleteToolCall(...)`
- but `onCompleteResponse(...).aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests()` may contain only the first tool call from a delta

This creates inconsistent history/memory: assistant `AiMessage` contains fewer tool requests than tool results produced for the same turn.

**Log and Stack trace**
No exception is thrown (logical/state mismatch, not a crash).

Observed callback sequence:

```text
onCompleteToolCall(index=0, id=tool-1, ...)
onCompleteToolCall(index=1, id=tool-2, ...)
onCompleteResponse.aiMessage.toolExecutionRequests.size=1
executedToolResults.size=2
```

Resulting history for that turn:

- assistant `AiMessage`: 1 tool request
- tool result messages: 2 entries

**To Reproduce**
Two minimal ways:

1) Black-box runtime repro (no code-heavy setup)

- Use any OpenAI-compatible streaming model/tool setup.
- Ask model to call tools in parallel, e.g.:
  - `Run tool run_sql for each query in parallel: SELECT 1, SELECT 2, ..., SELECT 7. Return only tool calls.`
- Observe:
  - multiple `onCompleteToolCall(...)` callbacks
  - final `onCompleteResponse(...).aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size()` can be smaller (often `1`) in affected versions.

2) Low-level unit-test repro (preferred for maintainers)

```java
package dev.langchain4j.model.openai;

import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;

import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.*;
import java.util.List;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;

class OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilderRegressionTest {

    @Test
    void should_keep_all_tool_calls_from_same_delta() {
        OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder builder = new OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder();

        ToolCall tc1 = ToolCall.builder()
                .id("call_1")
                .index(0)
                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
                .function(FunctionCall.builder().name("run_sql").arguments("{\"q\":\"SELECT 1\"}").build())
                .build();

        ToolCall tc2 = ToolCall.builder()
                .id("call_2")
                .index(1)
                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
                .function(FunctionCall.builder().name("run_sql").arguments("{\"q\":\"SELECT 2\"}").build())
                .build();

        ChatCompletionResponse partial = ChatCompletionResponse.builder()
                .id("resp_1")
                .model("openai-compatible-model")
                .choices(List.of(ChatCompletionChoice.builder()
                        .index(0)
                        .delta(Delta.builder().toolCalls(List.of(tc1, tc2)).build())
                        .build()))
                .build();

        builder.append(partial);
        ChatResponse response = builder.build();

        assertThat(response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests()).hasSize(2);
        assertThat(response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests())
                .extracting(it -> it.id())
                .containsExactly("call_1", "call_2");
    }
}
```

**Expected behavior**
`ChatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests()` must contain the same complete set of tool calls that were emitted/executed for that model turn.

**Please complete the following information:**
- LangChain4j version: `1.13.0-SNAPSHOT` (observed in current environment; likely affects versions with same `OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder.append` logic)
- LLM(s) used: Mistral via OpenAI-compatible API
- Java version: 17
- Spring Boot version (if applicable): N/A

**Additional context**
Likely root cause in affected versions is asymmetry between streaming callback handling and final response building:

- `OpenAiStreamingChatModel.handle(...)` iterates all `delta.toolCalls()`
- `OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder.append(...)` keeps only first tool call from a multi-call delta

Suggested fix:

- In `OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder.append(...)`, iterate all `delta.toolCalls()` entries and reuse existing per-entry accumulation logic.

Suggested regression test:

- Add a test in `OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilderTest`
- feed one streamed delta containing 2 tool calls
- assert final `aiMessage.toolExecutionRequests()` size is 2 and IDs/names/arguments for both entries are preserved

Possibly related:

- #4573
- #4528

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.openai;
     2	
     3	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrBlank;
     4	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrEmpty;
     5	import static dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.OpenAiUtils.finishReasonFrom;
     6	import static dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.OpenAiUtils.tokenUsageFrom;
     7	import static java.util.stream.Collectors.toList;
     8	
     9	import dev.langchain4j.Internal;
    10	import dev.langchain4j.agent.tool.ToolExecutionRequest;
    11	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
    12	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.SuccessfulHttpResponse;
    13	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.sse.ServerSentEvent;
    14	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
    15	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.ParsedAndRawResponse;
    16	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ChatCompletionChoice;
    17	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ChatCompletionResponse;
    18	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.Delta;
    19	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.FunctionCall;
    20	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ToolCall;
    21	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.completion.CompletionChoice;
    22	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.completion.CompletionResponse;
    23	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.shared.Usage;
    24	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
    25	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
    26	import java.util.ArrayList;
    27	import java.util.List;
    28	import java.util.Map;
    29	import java.util.Queue;
    30	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    31	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentLinkedQueue;
    32	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicInteger;
    33	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
    34	
    35	/**
    36	 * This class needs to be thread safe because it is called when a streaming result comes back
    37	 * and there is no guarantee that this thread will be the same as the one that initiated the request,
    38	 * in fact it almost certainly won't be.
    39	 */
    40	@Internal
    41	public class OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder {
    42	
    43	    private final StringBuffer contentBuilder = new StringBuffer();
    44	    private final StringBuffer reasoningContentBuilder;
    45	
    46	    private final StringBuffer toolNameBuilder = new StringBuffer(); // legacy
    47	    private final StringBuffer toolArgumentsBuilder = new StringBuffer(); // legacy
    48	
    49	    private final Map<Integer, ToolExecutionRequestBuilder> indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder =
    50	            new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    51	    private final AtomicInteger fallbackToolCallIndex = new AtomicInteger(0);
    52	
    53	    private final AtomicReference<String> id = new AtomicReference<>();
    54	    private final AtomicReference<Long> created = new AtomicReference<>();
    55	    private final AtomicReference<String> model = new AtomicReference<>();
    56	    private final AtomicReference<String> serviceTier = new AtomicReference<>();
    57	    private final AtomicReference<String> systemFingerprint = new AtomicReference<>();
    58	    private final AtomicReference<TokenUsage> tokenUsage = new AtomicReference<>();
    59	    private final AtomicReference<FinishReason> finishReason = new AtomicReference<>();
    60	    private final AtomicReference<SuccessfulHttpResponse> rawHttpResponse = new AtomicReference<>();
    61	    private final Queue<ServerSentEvent> rawServerSentEvents = new ConcurrentLinkedQueue<>();
    62	
    63	    private final boolean returnThinking;
    64	    private final boolean accumulateToolCallId;
    65	
    66	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder() {
    67	        this(false, true);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean returnThinking) {
    71	        this(returnThinking, true);
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean returnThinking, boolean accumulateToolCallId) {
    75	        this.returnThinking = returnThinking;
    76	        this.accumulateToolCallId = accumulateToolCallId;
    77	        if (returnThinking) {
    78	            this.reasoningContentBuilder = new StringBuffer();
    79	        } else {
    80	            this.reasoningContentBuilder = null;
    81	        }
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    public void append(ParsedAndRawResponse<ChatCompletionResponse> parsedAndRawResponse) {
    85	        if (parsedAndRawResponse != null) {
    86	            if (parsedAndRawResponse.rawHttpResponse() != null) {
    87	                rawHttpResponse.set(parsedAndRawResponse.rawHttpResponse());
    88	            }
    89	            if (parsedAndRawResponse.rawServerSentEvent() != null) {
    90	                rawServerSentEvents.add(parsedAndRawResponse.rawServerSentEvent());
    91	            }
    92	
    93	            append(parsedAndRawResponse.parsedResponse());
    94	        }
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    public void append(ChatCompletionResponse partialResponse) {
    98	        if (partialResponse == null) {
    99	            return;
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.id())) {
   103	            this.id.set(partialResponse.id());
   104	        }
   105	        if (partialResponse.created() != null) {
   106	            this.created.set(partialResponse.created());
   107	        }
   108	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.model())) {
   109	            this.model.set(partialResponse.model());
   110	        }
   111	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.serviceTier())) {
   112	            this.serviceTier.set(partialResponse.serviceTier());
   113	        }
   114	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.systemFingerprint())) {
   115	            this.systemFingerprint.set(partialResponse.systemFingerprint());
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        Usage usage = partialResponse.usage();
   119	        if (usage != null) {
   120	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsageFrom(usage));
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        List<ChatCompletionChoice> choices = partialResponse.choices();
   124	        if (isNullOrEmpty(choices)) {
   125	            return;
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        ChatCompletionChoice chatCompletionChoice = choices.get(0);
   129	        if (chatCompletionChoice == null) {
   130	            return;
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        String finishReason = chatCompletionChoice.finishReason();
   134	        if (finishReason != null) {
   135	            this.finishReason.set(finishReasonFrom(finishReason));
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        Delta delta = chatCompletionChoice.delta();
   139	        if (delta == null) {
   140	            return;
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        String content = delta.content();
   144	        if (!isNullOrEmpty(content)) {
   145	            this.contentBuilder.append(content);
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        String reasoningContent = delta.reasoningContent();
   149	        if (returnThinking && !isNullOrEmpty(reasoningContent)) {
   150	            this.reasoningContentBuilder.append(reasoningContent);
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        if (delta.functionCall() != null) {
   154	            FunctionCall functionCall = delta.functionCall();
   155	
   156	            if (functionCall.name() != null) {
   157	                this.toolNameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
   158	            }
   159	
   160	            if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
   161	                this.toolArgumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
   162	            }
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        if (delta.toolCalls() != null && !delta.toolCalls().isEmpty()) {
   166	            ToolCall toolCall = delta.toolCalls().get(0);
   167	            int toolCallIndex = toolCall.index() != null ? toolCall.index() : fallbackToolCallIndex.get();
   168	
   169	            ToolExecutionRequestBuilder builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
   170	                    toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
   171	
   172	            // When index is null and a different tool call id appears, increment the fallback index
   173	            if (toolCall.index() == null
   174	                    && toolCall.id() != null
   175	                    && !builder.idBuilder.isEmpty()
   176	                    && !builder.idBuilder.toString().equals(toolCall.id())) {
   177	                toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.incrementAndGet();
   178	                builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
   179	                        toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
   180	            }
   181	
   182	            if (toolCall.id() != null) {
   183	                if (accumulateToolCallId) {
   184	                    builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
   185	                } else {
   186	                    builder.idBuilder.setLength(0);
   187	                    builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
   188	                }
   189	            }
   190	
   191	            FunctionCall functionCall = toolCall.function();
   192	            if (functionCall.name() != null) {
   193	                builder.nameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
   194	            }
   195	            if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
   196	                builder.argumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
   197	            }
   198	        }
   199	    }
   200	
   201	    public void append(CompletionResponse partialResponse) {
   202	        if (partialResponse == null) {
   203	            return;
   204	        }
   205	
   206	        Usage usage = partialResponse.usage();
   207	        if (usage != null) {
   208	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsageFrom(usage));
   209	        }
   210	
   211	        List<CompletionChoice> choices = partialResponse.choices();
   212	        if (isNullOrEmpty(choices)) {
   213	            return;
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        CompletionChoice completionChoice = choices.get(0);
   217	        if (completionChoice == null) {
   218	            return;
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        String finishReason = completionChoice.finishReason();
   222	        if (finishReason != null) {
   223	            this.finishReason.set(finishReasonFrom(finishReason));
   224	        }
   225	
   226	        String token = completionChoice.text();
   227	        if (token != null) {
   228	            this.contentBuilder.append(token);
   229	        }
   230	    }
   231	
   232	    public ChatResponse build() {
   233	        return ChatResponse.builder()
   234	                .aiMessage(buildAiMessage())
   235	                .metadata(buildMetadata())
   236	                .build();
   237	    }
   238	
   239	    private AiMessage buildAiMessage() {
   240	        String text = contentBuilder.toString();
   241	
   242	        String thinking = null;
   243	        if (returnThinking) {
   244	            thinking = reasoningContentBuilder.toString();
   245	        }
   246	
   247	        return AiMessage.builder()
   248	                .text(isNullOrEmpty(text) ? null : text)
   249	                .thinking(isNullOrEmpty(thinking) ? null : thinking)
   250	                .toolExecutionRequests(buildToolExecutionRequests())
   251	                .build();
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    private List<ToolExecutionRequest> buildToolExecutionRequests() {
   255	        List<ToolExecutionRequest> toolExecutionRequests = new ArrayList<>();
   256	
   257	        // legacy
   258	        String toolName = toolNameBuilder.toString();
   259	        if (!toolName.isEmpty()) {
   260	            ToolExecutionRequest toolExecutionRequest = ToolExecutionRequest.builder()
   261	                    .name(toolName)
   262	                    .arguments(toolArgumentsBuilder.toString())
   263	                    .build();
   264	            toolExecutionRequests.add(toolExecutionRequest);
   265	        }
   266	
   267	        if (!indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.isEmpty()) {
   268	            List<ToolExecutionRequest> toolRequests = indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.values().stream()
   269	                    .map(it -> ToolExecutionRequest.builder()
   270	                            .id(it.idBuilder.toString())
   271	                            .name(it.nameBuilder.toString())
   272	                            .arguments(it.argumentsBuilder.toString())
   273	                            .build())
   274	                    .collect(toList());
   275	            toolExecutionRequests.addAll(toolRequests);
   276	        }
   277	
   278	        return toolExecutionRequests;
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    private OpenAiChatResponseMetadata buildMetadata() {
   282	        return OpenAiChatResponseMetadata.builder()
   283	                .id(id.get())
   284	                .modelName(model.get())
   285	                .tokenUsage(tokenUsage.get())
   286	                .finishReason(finishReason.get())
   287	                .created(created.get())
   288	                .serviceTier(serviceTier.get())
   289	                .systemFingerprint(systemFingerprint.get())
   290	                .rawHttpResponse(rawHttpResponse.get())
   291	                .rawServerSentEvents(new ArrayList<>(rawServerSentEvents))
   292	                .build();
   293	    }
   294	
   295	    private static class ToolExecutionRequestBuilder {
   296	
   297	        private final StringBuffer idBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   298	        private final StringBuffer nameBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   299	        private final StringBuffer argumentsBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   300	    }
   301	}

    43	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ChatCompletionResponse;
    44	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.Delta;
    45	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ToolCall;
    46	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.shared.StreamOptions;
    47	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.spi.OpenAiStreamingChatModelBuilderFactory;
    48	import java.time.Duration;
    49	import java.util.List;
    50	import java.util.Map;
    51	import java.util.function.Supplier;
    52	import org.slf4j.Logger;
    53	
    54	/**
    55	 * Represents an OpenAI language model with a chat completion interface, such as gpt-4o-mini and o3.
    56	 * The model's response is streamed token by token and should be handled with {@link StreamingResponseHandler}.
    57	 * You can find description of parameters <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/chat/create">here</a>.
    58	 */
    59	public class OpenAiStreamingChatModel implements StreamingChatModel {
    60	
    61	    private final OpenAiClient client;
    62	    private final OpenAiChatRequestParameters defaultRequestParameters;
    63	    private final boolean strictJsonSchema;
    64	    private final boolean strictTools;
    65	    private final boolean returnThinking;
    66	    private final boolean sendThinking;
    67	    private final String thinkingFieldName;
    68	    private final boolean accumulateToolCallId;
    69	    private final List<ChatModelListener> listeners;
    70	
    71	    public OpenAiStreamingChatModel(OpenAiStreamingChatModelBuilder builder) {
    72	        this.client = OpenAiClient.builder()
    73	                .httpClientBuilder(builder.httpClientBuilder)
    74	                .baseUrl(getOrDefault(builder.baseUrl, DEFAULT_OPENAI_URL))
    75	                .apiKey(builder.apiKey)
    76	                .organizationId(builder.organizationId)
    77	                .projectId(builder.projectId)
    78	                .connectTimeout(getOrDefault(builder.timeout, ofSeconds(15)))
    79	                .readTimeout(getOrDefault(builder.timeout, ofSeconds(60)))
    80	                .logRequests(getOrDefault(builder.logRequests, false))
    81	                .logResponses(getOrDefault(builder.logResponses, false))
    82	                .logger(builder.logger)
    83	                .userAgent(DEFAULT_USER_AGENT)
    84	                .customHeaders(builder.customHeadersSupplier)
    85	                .customQueryParams(builder.customQueryParams)
    86	                .build();
    87	
    88	        ChatRequestParameters commonParameters;
    89	        if (builder.defaultRequestParameters != null) {
    90	            validate(builder.defaultRequestParameters);
    91	            commonParameters = builder.defaultRequestParameters;
    92	        } else {
    93	            commonParameters = DefaultChatRequestParameters.EMPTY;
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        OpenAiChatRequestParameters openAiParameters;
    97	        if (builder.defaultRequestParameters instanceof OpenAiChatRequestParameters openAiChatRequestParameters) {
    98	            openAiParameters = openAiChatRequestParameters;
    99	        } else {
   100	            openAiParameters = OpenAiChatRequestParameters.EMPTY;
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        this.defaultRequestParameters = OpenAiChatRequestParameters.builder()
   104	                // common parameters
   105	                .modelName(getOrDefault(builder.modelName, commonParameters.modelName()))
   106	                .temperature(getOrDefault(builder.temperature, commonParameters.temperature()))
   107	                .topP(getOrDefault(builder.topP, commonParameters.topP()))
   108	                .frequencyPenalty(getOrDefault(builder.frequencyPenalty, commonParameters.frequencyPenalty()))
   109	                .presencePenalty(getOrDefault(builder.presencePenalty, commonParameters.presencePenalty()))
   110	                .maxOutputTokens(getOrDefault(builder.maxTokens, commonParameters.maxOutputTokens()))
   111	                .stopSequences(getOrDefault(builder.stop, commonParameters.stopSequences()))
   112	                .toolSpecifications(commonParameters.toolSpecifications())
   113	                .toolChoice(commonParameters.toolChoice())
   114	                .responseFormat(getOrDefault(builder.responseFormat, commonParameters.responseFormat()))
   115	                // OpenAI-specific parameters
   116	                .maxCompletionTokens(getOrDefault(builder.maxCompletionTokens, openAiParameters.maxCompletionTokens()))
   117	                .logitBias(getOrDefault(builder.logitBias, openAiParameters.logitBias()))
   118	                .parallelToolCalls(getOrDefault(builder.parallelToolCalls, openAiParameters.parallelToolCalls()))
   119	                .seed(getOrDefault(builder.seed, openAiParameters.seed()))
   120	                .user(getOrDefault(builder.user, openAiParameters.user()))
   121	                .store(getOrDefault(builder.store, openAiParameters.store()))
   122	                .metadata(getOrDefault(builder.metadata, openAiParameters.metadata()))
   123	                .serviceTier(getOrDefault(builder.serviceTier, openAiParameters.serviceTier()))
   124	                .reasoningEffort(getOrDefault(builder.reasoningEffort, openAiParameters.reasoningEffort()))
   125	                .customParameters(getOrDefault(builder.customParameters, openAiParameters.customParameters()))
   126	                .build();
   127	        this.strictJsonSchema = getOrDefault(builder.strictJsonSchema, false);
   128	        this.strictTools = getOrDefault(builder.strictTools, false);
   129	        this.returnThinking = getOrDefault(builder.returnThinking, false);
   130	        this.sendThinking = getOrDefault(builder.sendThinking, false);
   131	        this.thinkingFieldName = getOrDefault(builder.thinkingFieldName, "reasoning_content");
   132	        this.accumulateToolCallId = getOrDefault(builder.accumulateToolCallId, true);
   133	        this.listeners = copy(builder.listeners);
   134	    }
   135	
   136	    @Override
   137	    public OpenAiChatRequestParameters defaultRequestParameters() {
   138	        return defaultRequestParameters;
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    @Override
   142	    public void doChat(ChatRequest chatRequest, StreamingChatResponseHandler handler) {
   143	
   144	        OpenAiChatRequestParameters parameters = (OpenAiChatRequestParameters) chatRequest.parameters();
   145	        validate(parameters);
   146	
   147	        ChatCompletionRequest openAiRequest =
   148	                toOpenAiChatRequest(
   149	                                chatRequest, parameters, sendThinking, thinkingFieldName, strictTools, strictJsonSchema)
   150	                        .stream(true)
   151	                        .streamOptions(
   152	                                StreamOptions.builder().includeUsage(true).build())
   153	                        .build();
   154	
   155	        OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder openAiResponseBuilder =
   156	                new OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder(returnThinking, accumulateToolCallId);
   157	        ToolCallBuilder toolCallBuilder = new ToolCallBuilder();
   158	
   159	        client.chatCompletion(openAiRequest)
   160	                .onRawPartialResponse(parsedAndRawResponse -> {
   161	                    openAiResponseBuilder.append(parsedAndRawResponse);
   162	                    handle(parsedAndRawResponse, toolCallBuilder, handler);
   163	                })
   164	                .onComplete(() -> {
   165	                    if (toolCallBuilder.hasRequests()) {
   166	                        onCompleteToolCall(handler, toolCallBuilder.buildAndReset());
   167	                    }
   168	
   169	                    ChatResponse completeResponse = openAiResponseBuilder.build();
   170	                    onCompleteResponse(handler, completeResponse);
   171	                })
   172	                .onError(throwable -> {
   173	                    RuntimeException mappedException = ExceptionMapper.DEFAULT.mapException(throwable);
   174	                    withLoggingExceptions(() -> handler.onError(mappedException));
   175	                })
   176	                .execute();
   177	    }
   178	
   179	    private void handle(
   180	            ParsedAndRawResponse<ChatCompletionResponse> parsedAndRawResponse,
   181	            ToolCallBuilder toolCallBuilder,
   182	            StreamingChatResponseHandler handler) {
   183	        ChatCompletionResponse partialResponse = parsedAndRawResponse.parsedResponse();
   184	        if (partialResponse == null) {
   185	            return;
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        List<ChatCompletionChoice> choices = partialResponse.choices();
   189	        if (isNullOrEmpty(choices)) {
   190	            return;
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        ChatCompletionChoice chatCompletionChoice = choices.get(0);
   194	        if (chatCompletionChoice == null) {
   195	            return;
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        Delta delta = chatCompletionChoice.delta();
   199	        if (delta == null) {
   200	            return;
   201	        }
   202	
   203	        String content = delta.content();
   204	        if (!isNullOrEmpty(content)) {
   205	            onPartialResponse(handler, content, parsedAndRawResponse.streamingHandle());
   206	        }
   207	
   208	        String reasoningContent = delta.reasoningContent();
   209	        if (returnThinking && !isNullOrEmpty(reasoningContent)) {
   210	            onPartialThinking(handler, reasoningContent, parsedAndRawResponse.streamingHandle());
   211	        }
   212	
   213	        List<ToolCall> toolCalls = delta.toolCalls();
   214	        if (toolCalls != null) {
   215	            for (ToolCall toolCall : toolCalls) {
   216	
   217	                int index;
   218	                if (toolCall.index() != null) {
   219	                    index = toolCall.index();
   220	                } else {
   221	                    index = toolCallBuilder.index();
   222	                    // When index is null and a different tool call id appears, increment the index
   223	                    if (toolCall.id() != null
   224	                            && toolCallBuilder.id() != null
   225	                            && !toolCallBuilder.id().equals(toolCall.id())) {
   226	                        index = toolCallBuilder.index() + 1;
   227	                    }
   228	                }
   229	                if (toolCallBuilder.index() != index) {
   230	                    onCompleteToolCall(handler, toolCallBuilder.buildAndReset());
   231	                    toolCallBuilder.updateIndex(index);
   232	                }
   233	
   234	                String id = toolCallBuilder.updateId(toolCall.id());
   235	                String name = toolCallBuilder.updateName(toolCall.function().name());
   236	
   237	                String partialArguments = toolCall.function().arguments();
   238	                if (isNotNullOrEmpty(partialArguments)) {
   239	                    toolCallBuilder.appendArguments(partialArguments);
   240	
   241	                    PartialToolCall partialToolRequest = PartialToolCall.builder()
   242	                            .index(index)
   243	                            .id(id)
   244	                            .name(name)
   245	                            .partialArguments(partialArguments)
   246	                            .build();
   247	                    onPartialToolCall(handler, partialToolRequest, parsedAndRawResponse.streamingHandle());
   248	                }
   249	            }
   250	        }
   251	    }
   252	
   253	    @Override
   254	    public List<ChatModelListener> listeners() {
   255	        return listeners;
   256	    }
   257	
   258	    @Override
   259	    public ModelProvider provider() {
   260	        return OPEN_AI;
   261	    }
   262	
   263	    public static OpenAiStreamingChatModelBuilder builder() {
   264	        for (OpenAiStreamingChatModelBuilderFactory factory :
   265	                loadFactories(OpenAiStreamingChatModelBuilderFactory.class)) {
   266	            return factory.get();
   267	        }
   268	        return new OpenAiStreamingChatModelBuilder();
   269	    }

     2	
     3	import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;
     4	
     5	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
     6	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.*;

     9	
    10	class OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilderTest {
    11	
    12	    @Test
    13	    void should_handle_null_tool_call_index() {
    14	        // Given: a tool call with null index (as Gemini's OpenAI-compatible API returns)
    15	        OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder builder = new OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder();
    16	
    17	        ToolCall toolCall = ToolCall.builder()
    18	                .id("call_123")
    19	                .index(null)
    20	                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
    21	                .function(FunctionCall.builder()
    22	                        .name("getWeather")
    23	                        .arguments("{\"city\": \"Berlin\"}")
    24	                        .build())
    25	                .build();
    26	
    27	        ChatCompletionResponse response = chatCompletionResponse(toolCall);
    28	
    29	        // When: appending the response (should not throw NPE)
    30	        builder.append(response);
    31	
    32	        // Then: the tool execution request is built correctly
    33	        ChatResponse chatResponse = builder.build();
    34	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests()).hasSize(1);
    35	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().get(0).name())
    36	                .isEqualTo("getWeather");
    37	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().get(0).arguments())
    38	                .isEqualTo("{\"city\": \"Berlin\"}");
    39	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().get(0).id()).isEqualTo("call_123");
    40	    }
    41	
    42	    @Test
    43	    void should_handle_multiple_tool_calls_with_null_index() {
    44	        // Given: two distinct tool calls, both with null index (Gemini parallel tool calls)
    45	        OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder builder = new OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder();
    46	
    47	        // First tool call streaming chunks
    48	        ToolCall firstToolCall = ToolCall.builder()
    49	                .id("call_aaa")
    50	                .index(null)
    51	                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
    52	                .function(FunctionCall.builder()
    53	                        .name("getWeather")
    54	                        .arguments("{\"city\": \"Berlin\"}")
    55	                        .build())
    56	                .build();
    57	        builder.append(chatCompletionResponse(firstToolCall));
    58	
    59	        // Second tool call streaming chunks — different id, still null index
    60	        ToolCall secondToolCall = ToolCall.builder()
    61	                .id("call_bbb")
    62	                .index(null)
    63	                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
    64	                .function(FunctionCall.builder()
    65	                        .name("getTemperature")
    66	                        .arguments("{\"city\": \"Paris\"}")
    67	                        .build())
    68	                .build();
    69	        builder.append(chatCompletionResponse(secondToolCall));
    70	
    71	        // Then: both tool execution requests should be built separately
    72	        ChatResponse chatResponse = builder.build();
    73	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests()).hasSize(2);
    74	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().get(0).name())
    75	                .isEqualTo("getWeather");
    76	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().get(0).id()).isEqualTo("call_aaa");
    77	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().get(1).name())
    78	                .isEqualTo("getTemperature");
    79	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().get(1).id()).isEqualTo("call_bbb");
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    @Test
    83	    void should_handle_non_null_tool_call_index() {
    84	        // Given: a standard tool call with non-null index
    85	        OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder builder = new OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder();
    86	
    87	        ToolCall toolCall = ToolCall.builder()
    88	                .id("call_456")
    89	                .index(0)
    90	                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
    91	                .function(FunctionCall.builder()
    92	                        .name("getTemperature")
    93	                        .arguments("{\"city\": \"Paris\"}")
    94	                        .build())
    95	                .build();
    96	
    97	        builder.append(chatCompletionResponse(toolCall));
    98	
    99	        // Then
   100	        ChatResponse chatResponse = builder.build();
   101	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests()).hasSize(1);
   102	        assertThat(chatResponse.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().get(0).name())
   103	                .isEqualTo("getTemperature");
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    private static ChatCompletionResponse chatCompletionResponse(ToolCall toolCall) {
   107	        return ChatCompletionResponse.builder()
   108	                .id("resp_1")
   109	                .model("gemini-2.0-flash")
   110	                .choices(List.of(ChatCompletionChoice.builder()
   111	                        .index(0)
   112	                        .delta(Delta.builder().toolCalls(List.of(toolCall)).build())
   113	                        .build()))
   114	                .build();
   115	    }
   116	}

package dev.langchain4j.model.openai;

import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;

import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.*;
import java.util.List;

public class ReproTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder builder = new OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder();

        ToolCall tc1 = ToolCall.builder()
                .id("call_1")
                .index(0)
                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
                .function(FunctionCall.builder().name("run_sql").arguments("{\"q\":\"SELECT 1\"}").build())
                .build();

        ToolCall tc2 = ToolCall.builder()
                .id("call_2")
                .index(1)
                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
                .function(FunctionCall.builder().name("run_sql").arguments("{\"q\":\"SELECT 2\"}").build())
                .build();

        ChatCompletionResponse partial = ChatCompletionResponse.builder()
                .id("resp_1")
                .model("openai-compatible-model")
                .choices(List.of(ChatCompletionChoice.builder()
                        .index(0)
                        .delta(Delta.builder().toolCalls(List.of(tc1, tc2)).build())
                        .build()))
                .build();

        builder.append(partial);
        ChatResponse response = builder.build();

        System.out.println("Tool execution requests size: " + response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size());
        System.out.println("Expected: 2");
        
        if (response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size() == 2) {
            System.out.println("PASS: Got correct number of tool calls");
        } else {
            System.out.println("FAIL: Expected 2 but got " + response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size());
            System.exit(1);
        }
        
        assertThat(response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests()).hasSize(2);
        assertThat(response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests())
                .extracting(it -> it.id())
                .containsExactly("call_1", "call_2");
        System.out.println("All assertions passed!");
    }
}

     7	import static java.util.stream.Collectors.toList;
     8	
     9	import dev.langchain4j.Internal;
    10	import dev.langchain4j.agent.tool.ToolExecutionRequest;
    11	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
    12	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.SuccessfulHttpResponse;
    13	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.sse.ServerSentEvent;
    14	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
    15	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.ParsedAndRawResponse;
    16	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ChatCompletionChoice;
    17	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ChatCompletionResponse;
    18	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.Delta;
    19	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.FunctionCall;
    20	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ToolCall;
    21	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.completion.CompletionChoice;
    22	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.completion.CompletionResponse;
    23	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.shared.Usage;
    24	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
    25	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
    26	import java.util.ArrayList;
    27	import java.util.List;
    28	import java.util.Map;
    29	import java.util.Queue;
    30	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    31	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentLinkedQueue;
    32	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicInteger;
    33	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
    34	
    35	/**
    36	 * This class needs to be thread safe because it is called when a streaming result comes back
    37	 * and there is no guarantee that this thread will be the same as the one that initiated the request,
    38	 * in fact it almost certainly won't be.
    39	 */
    40	@Internal
    41	public class OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder {
    42	
    43	    private final StringBuffer contentBuilder = new StringBuffer();
    44	    private final StringBuffer reasoningContentBuilder;
    45	
    46	    private final StringBuffer toolNameBuilder = new StringBuffer(); // legacy
    47	    private final StringBuffer toolArgumentsBuilder = new StringBuffer(); // legacy
    48	
    49	    private final Map<Integer, ToolExecutionRequestBuilder> indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder =
    50	            new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    51	    private final AtomicInteger fallbackToolCallIndex = new AtomicInteger(0);
    52	
    53	    private final AtomicReference<String> id = new AtomicReference<>();
    54	    private final AtomicReference<Long> created = new AtomicReference<>();
    55	    private final AtomicReference<String> model = new AtomicReference<>();
    56	    private final AtomicReference<String> serviceTier = new AtomicReference<>();
    57	    private final AtomicReference<String> systemFingerprint = new AtomicReference<>();
    58	    private final AtomicReference<TokenUsage> tokenUsage = new AtomicReference<>();
    59	    private final AtomicReference<FinishReason> finishReason = new AtomicReference<>();
    60	    private final AtomicReference<SuccessfulHttpResponse> rawHttpResponse = new AtomicReference<>();
    61	    private final Queue<ServerSentEvent> rawServerSentEvents = new ConcurrentLinkedQueue<>();
    62	
    63	    private final boolean returnThinking;
    64	    private final boolean accumulateToolCallId;
    65	
    66	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder() {
    67	        this(false, true);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean returnThinking) {
    71	        this(returnThinking, true);
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean returnThinking, boolean accumulateToolCallId) {
    75	        this.returnThinking = returnThinking;
    76	        this.accumulateToolCallId = accumulateToolCallId;
    77	        if (returnThinking) {
    78	            this.reasoningContentBuilder = new StringBuffer();
    79	        } else {
    80	            this.reasoningContentBuilder = null;
    81	        }
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    public void append(ParsedAndRawResponse<ChatCompletionResponse> parsedAndRawResponse) {
    85	        if (parsedAndRawResponse != null) {
    86	            if (parsedAndRawResponse.rawHttpResponse() != null) {
    87	                rawHttpResponse.set(parsedAndRawResponse.rawHttpResponse());
    88	            }
    89	            if (parsedAndRawResponse.rawServerSentEvent() != null) {
    90	                rawServerSentEvents.add(parsedAndRawResponse.rawServerSentEvent());
    91	            }
    92	
    93	            append(parsedAndRawResponse.parsedResponse());
    94	        }
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    public void append(ChatCompletionResponse partialResponse) {
    98	        if (partialResponse == null) {
    99	            return;
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.id())) {
   103	            this.id.set(partialResponse.id());
   104	        }
   105	        if (partialResponse.created() != null) {
   106	            this.created.set(partialResponse.created());
   107	        }
   108	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.model())) {
   109	            this.model.set(partialResponse.model());
   110	        }
   111	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.serviceTier())) {
   112	            this.serviceTier.set(partialResponse.serviceTier());
   113	        }
   114	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.systemFingerprint())) {
   115	            this.systemFingerprint.set(partialResponse.systemFingerprint());
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        Usage usage = partialResponse.usage();
   119	        if (usage != null) {
   120	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsageFrom(usage));
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        List<ChatCompletionChoice> choices = partialResponse.choices();
   124	        if (isNullOrEmpty(choices)) {
   125	            return;
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        ChatCompletionChoice chatCompletionChoice = choices.get(0);
   129	        if (chatCompletionChoice == null) {
   130	            return;
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        String finishReason = chatCompletionChoice.finishReason();
   134	        if (finishReason != null) {
   135	            this.finishReason.set(finishReasonFrom(finishReason));
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        Delta delta = chatCompletionChoice.delta();
   139	        if (delta == null) {
   140	            return;
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        String content = delta.content();
   144	        if (!isNullOrEmpty(content)) {
   145	            this.contentBuilder.append(content);
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        String reasoningContent = delta.reasoningContent();
   149	        if (returnThinking && !isNullOrEmpty(reasoningContent)) {
   150	            this.reasoningContentBuilder.append(reasoningContent);
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        if (delta.functionCall() != null) {
   154	            FunctionCall functionCall = delta.functionCall();
   155	
   156	            if (functionCall.name() != null) {
   157	                this.toolNameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
   158	            }
   159	
   160	            if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
   161	                this.toolArgumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
   162	            }
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        if (delta.toolCalls() != null && !delta.toolCalls().isEmpty()) {
   166	            ToolCall toolCall = delta.toolCalls().get(0);
   167	            int toolCallIndex = toolCall.index() != null ? toolCall.index() : fallbackToolCallIndex.get();
   168	
   169	            ToolExecutionRequestBuilder builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
   170	                    toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
   171	
   172	            // When index is null and a different tool call id appears, increment the fallback index
   173	            if (toolCall.index() == null
   174	                    && toolCall.id() != null
   175	                    && !builder.idBuilder.isEmpty()
   176	                    && !builder.idBuilder.toString().equals(toolCall.id())) {
   177	                toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.incrementAndGet();
   178	                builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
   179	                        toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
   180	            }
   181	
   182	            if (toolCall.id() != null) {
   183	                if (accumulateToolCallId) {
   184	                    builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
   185	                } else {
   186	                    builder.idBuilder.setLength(0);
   187	                    builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
   188	                }
   189	            }
   190	
   191	            FunctionCall functionCall = toolCall.function();
   192	            if (functionCall.name() != null) {
   193	                builder.nameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
   194	            }
   195	            if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
   196	                builder.argumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
   197	            }
   198	        }
   199	    }
   200	
   201	    public void append(CompletionResponse partialResponse) {
   202	        if (partialResponse == null) {
   203	            return;
   204	        }
   205	
   206	        Usage usage = partialResponse.usage();
   207	        if (usage != null) {
   208	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsageFrom(usage));
   209	        }
   210	
   211	        List<CompletionChoice> choices = partialResponse.choices();
   212	        if (isNullOrEmpty(choices)) {
   213	            return;
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        CompletionChoice completionChoice = choices.get(0);
   217	        if (completionChoice == null) {
   218	            return;
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        String finishReason = completionChoice.finishReason();
   222	        if (finishReason != null) {
   223	            this.finishReason.set(finishReasonFrom(finishReason));
   224	        }
   225	
   226	        String token = completionChoice.text();
   227	        if (token != null) {
   228	            this.contentBuilder.append(token);
   229	        }
   230	    }
   231	
   232	    public ChatResponse build() {
   233	        return ChatResponse.builder()
   234	                .aiMessage(buildAiMessage())
   235	                .metadata(buildMetadata())
   236	                .build();
   237	    }
   238	
   239	    private AiMessage buildAiMessage() {
   240	        String text = contentBuilder.toString();
   241	
   242	        String thinking = null;
   243	        if (returnThinking) {
   244	            thinking = reasoningContentBuilder.toString();
   245	        }
   246	
   247	        return AiMessage.builder()
   248	                .text(isNullOrEmpty(text) ? null : text)
   249	                .thinking(isNullOrEmpty(thinking) ? null : thinking)
   250	                .toolExecutionRequests(buildToolExecutionRequests())
   251	                .build();
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    private List<ToolExecutionRequest> buildToolExecutionRequests() {
   255	        List<ToolExecutionRequest> toolExecutionRequests = new ArrayList<>();
   256	
   257	        // legacy
   258	        String toolName = toolNameBuilder.toString();
   259	        if (!toolName.isEmpty()) {
   260	            ToolExecutionRequest toolExecutionRequest = ToolExecutionRequest.builder()
   261	                    .name(toolName)
   262	                    .arguments(toolArgumentsBuilder.toString())
   263	                    .build();
   264	            toolExecutionRequests.add(toolExecutionRequest);
   265	        }
   266	
   267	        if (!indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.isEmpty()) {
   268	            List<ToolExecutionRequest> toolRequests = indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.values().stream()
   269	                    .map(it -> ToolExecutionRequest.builder()
   270	                            .id(it.idBuilder.toString())
   271	                            .name(it.nameBuilder.toString())
   272	                            .arguments(it.argumentsBuilder.toString())
   273	                            .build())
   274	                    .collect(toList());
   275	            toolExecutionRequests.addAll(toolRequests);
   276	        }
   277	
   278	        return toolExecutionRequests;
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    private OpenAiChatResponseMetadata buildMetadata() {
   282	        return OpenAiChatResponseMetadata.builder()
   283	                .id(id.get())
   284	                .modelName(model.get())
   285	                .tokenUsage(tokenUsage.get())
   286	                .finishReason(finishReason.get())
   287	                .created(created.get())
   288	                .serviceTier(serviceTier.get())
   289	                .systemFingerprint(systemFingerprint.get())
   290	                .rawHttpResponse(rawHttpResponse.get())
   291	                .rawServerSentEvents(new ArrayList<>(rawServerSentEvents))
   292	                .build();
   293	    }
   294	
   295	    private static class ToolExecutionRequestBuilder {
   296	
   297	        private final StringBuffer idBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   298	        private final StringBuffer nameBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   299	        private final StringBuffer argumentsBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   300	    }
   301	}

   253	    }
   254	
   255	    private List<ToolExecutionRequest> buildToolExecutionRequests() {
   256	        List<ToolExecutionRequest> toolExecutionRequests = new ArrayList<>();
   257	
   258	        // legacy
   259	        String toolName = toolNameBuilder.toString();
   260	        if (!toolName.isEmpty()) {
   261	            ToolExecutionRequest toolExecutionRequest = ToolExecutionRequest.builder()
   262	                    .name(toolName)
   263	                    .arguments(toolArgumentsBuilder.toString())
   264	                    .build();
   265	            toolExecutionRequests.add(toolExecutionRequest);
   266	        }
   267	
   268	        if (!indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.isEmpty()) {
   269	            List<ToolExecutionRequest> toolRequests = indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.values().stream()
   270	                    .map(it -> ToolExecutionRequest.builder()
   271	                            .id(it.idBuilder.toString())
   272	                            .name(it.nameBuilder.toString())
   273	                            .arguments(it.argumentsBuilder.toString())
   274	                            .build())
   275	                    .collect(toList());
   276	            toolExecutionRequests.addAll(toolRequests);
   277	        }
   278	
   279	        return toolExecutionRequests;
   280	    }
   281	
   282	    private OpenAiChatResponseMetadata buildMetadata() {
   283	        return OpenAiChatResponseMetadata.builder()
   284	                .id(id.get())
   285	                .modelName(model.get())
   286	                .tokenUsage(tokenUsage.get())
   287	                .finishReason(finishReason.get())
   288	                .created(created.get())
   289	                .serviceTier(serviceTier.get())
   290	                .systemFingerprint(systemFingerprint.get())
   291	                .rawHttpResponse(rawHttpResponse.get())
   292	                .rawServerSentEvents(new ArrayList<>(rawServerSentEvents))
   293	                .build();
   294	    }
   295	
   296	    private static class ToolExecutionRequestBuilder {
   297	
   298	        private final StringBuffer idBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   299	        private final StringBuffer nameBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   300	        private final StringBuffer argumentsBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   301	    }

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.openai;
     2	
     3	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrBlank;
     4	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrEmpty;
     5	import static dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.OpenAiUtils.finishReasonFrom;
     6	import static dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.OpenAiUtils.tokenUsageFrom;
     7	import static java.util.stream.Collectors.toList;
     8	
     9	import dev.langchain4j.Internal;
    10	import dev.langchain4j.agent.tool.ToolExecutionRequest;
    11	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
    12	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.SuccessfulHttpResponse;
    13	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.sse.ServerSentEvent;
    14	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
    15	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.ParsedAndRawResponse;
    16	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ChatCompletionChoice;
    17	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ChatCompletionResponse;
    18	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.Delta;
    19	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.FunctionCall;
    20	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ToolCall;
    21	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.completion.CompletionChoice;
    22	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.completion.CompletionResponse;
    23	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.shared.Usage;
    24	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
    25	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
    26	import java.util.ArrayList;
    27	import java.util.List;
    28	import java.util.Map;
    29	import java.util.Queue;
    30	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    31	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentLinkedQueue;
    32	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicInteger;
    33	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
    34	
    35	/**
    36	 * This class needs to be thread safe because it is called when a streaming result comes back
    37	 * and there is no guarantee that this thread will be the same as the one that initiated the request,
    38	 * in fact it almost certainly won't be.
    39	 */
    40	@Internal
    41	public class OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder {
    42	
    43	    private final StringBuffer contentBuilder = new StringBuffer();
    44	    private final StringBuffer reasoningContentBuilder;
    45	
    46	    private final StringBuffer toolNameBuilder = new StringBuffer(); // legacy
    47	    private final StringBuffer toolArgumentsBuilder = new StringBuffer(); // legacy
    48	
    49	    private final Map<Integer, ToolExecutionRequestBuilder> indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder =
    50	            new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    51	    private final AtomicInteger fallbackToolCallIndex = new AtomicInteger(0);
    52	
    53	    private final AtomicReference<String> id = new AtomicReference<>();
    54	    private final AtomicReference<Long> created = new AtomicReference<>();
    55	    private final AtomicReference<String> model = new AtomicReference<>();
    56	    private final AtomicReference<String> serviceTier = new AtomicReference<>();
    57	    private final AtomicReference<String> systemFingerprint = new AtomicReference<>();
    58	    private final AtomicReference<TokenUsage> tokenUsage = new AtomicReference<>();
    59	    private final AtomicReference<FinishReason> finishReason = new AtomicReference<>();
    60	    private final AtomicReference<SuccessfulHttpResponse> rawHttpResponse = new AtomicReference<>();
    61	    private final Queue<ServerSentEvent> rawServerSentEvents = new ConcurrentLinkedQueue<>();
    62	
    63	    private final boolean returnThinking;
    64	    private final boolean accumulateToolCallId;
    65	
    66	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder() {
    67	        this(false, true);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean returnThinking) {
    71	        this(returnThinking, true);
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean returnThinking, boolean accumulateToolCallId) {
    75	        this.returnThinking = returnThinking;
    76	        this.accumulateToolCallId = accumulateToolCallId;
    77	        if (returnThinking) {
    78	            this.reasoningContentBuilder = new StringBuffer();
    79	        } else {
    80	            this.reasoningContentBuilder = null;
    81	        }
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    public void append(ParsedAndRawResponse<ChatCompletionResponse> parsedAndRawResponse) {
    85	        if (parsedAndRawResponse != null) {
    86	            if (parsedAndRawResponse.rawHttpResponse() != null) {
    87	                rawHttpResponse.set(parsedAndRawResponse.rawHttpResponse());
    88	            }
    89	            if (parsedAndRawResponse.rawServerSentEvent() != null) {
    90	                rawServerSentEvents.add(parsedAndRawResponse.rawServerSentEvent());
    91	            }
    92	
    93	            append(parsedAndRawResponse.parsedResponse());
    94	        }
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    public void append(ChatCompletionResponse partialResponse) {
    98	        if (partialResponse == null) {
    99	            return;
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.id())) {
   103	            this.id.set(partialResponse.id());
   104	        }
   105	        if (partialResponse.created() != null) {
   106	            this.created.set(partialResponse.created());
   107	        }
   108	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.model())) {
   109	            this.model.set(partialResponse.model());
   110	        }
   111	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.serviceTier())) {
   112	            this.serviceTier.set(partialResponse.serviceTier());
   113	        }
   114	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.systemFingerprint())) {
   115	            this.systemFingerprint.set(partialResponse.systemFingerprint());
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        Usage usage = partialResponse.usage();
   119	        if (usage != null) {
   120	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsageFrom(usage));
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        List<ChatCompletionChoice> choices = partialResponse.choices();
   124	        if (isNullOrEmpty(choices)) {
   125	            return;
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        ChatCompletionChoice chatCompletionChoice = choices.get(0);
   129	        if (chatCompletionChoice == null) {
   130	            return;
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        String finishReason = chatCompletionChoice.finishReason();
   134	        if (finishReason != null) {
   135	            this.finishReason.set(finishReasonFrom(finishReason));
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        Delta delta = chatCompletionChoice.delta();
   139	        if (delta == null) {
   140	            return;
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        String content = delta.content();
   144	        if (!isNullOrEmpty(content)) {
   145	            this.contentBuilder.append(content);
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        String reasoningContent = delta.reasoningContent();
   149	        if (returnThinking && !isNullOrEmpty(reasoningContent)) {
   150	            this.reasoningContentBuilder.append(reasoningContent);
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        if (delta.functionCall() != null) {
   154	            FunctionCall functionCall = delta.functionCall();
   155	
   156	            if (functionCall.name() != null) {
   157	                this.toolNameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
   158	            }
   159	
   160	            if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
   161	                this.toolArgumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
   162	            }
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        
   166	if (delta.toolCalls() != null && !delta.toolCalls().isEmpty()) {
   167	            for (ToolCall toolCall : delta.toolCalls()) {
   168	                int toolCallIndex = toolCall.index() != null ? toolCall.index() : fallbackToolCallIndex.get();
   169	
   170	            ToolExecutionRequestBuilder builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
   171	                    toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
   172	
   173	            // When index is null and a different tool call id appears, increment the fallback index
   174	            if (toolCall.index() == null
   175	                    && toolCall.id() != null
   176	                    && !builder.idBuilder.isEmpty()
   177	                    && !builder.idBuilder.toString().equals(toolCall.id())) {
   178	                toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.incrementAndGet();
   179	                builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
   180	                        toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
   181	            }
   182	
   183	            if (toolCall.id() != null) {
   184	                if (accumulateToolCallId) {
   185	                    builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
   186	                } else {
   187	                    builder.idBuilder.setLength(0);
   188	                    builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
   189	                }
   190	            }
   191	
   192	            FunctionCall functionCall = toolCall.function();
   193	            if (functionCall.name() != null) {
   194	                builder.nameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
   195	            }
   196	            if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
   197	                builder.argumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
   198	            }
   199	        }
   200	    }

use strict;
use warnings;

my $file = 'langchain4j-open-ai/src/main/java/dev/langchain4j/model/openai/OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder.java';

open(my $fh, '<', $file) or die "Cannot open $file: $!";
my $content = do { local $/; <$fh> };
close($fh);

# The exact old string to replace (lines 165-198)
my $old = '        if (delta.toolCalls() != null && !delta.toolCalls().isEmpty()) {
            ToolCall toolCall = delta.toolCalls().get(0);
            int toolCallIndex = toolCall.index() != null ? toolCall.index() : fallbackToolCallIndex.get();

            ToolExecutionRequestBuilder builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
                    toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());

            // When index is null and a different tool call id appears, increment the fallback index
            if (toolCall.index() == null
                    && toolCall.id() != null
                    && !builder.idBuilder.isEmpty()
                    && !builder.idBuilder.toString().equals(toolCall.id())) {
                toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.incrementAndGet();
                builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
                        toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
            }

            if (toolCall.id() != null) {
                if (accumulateToolCallId) {
                    builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
                } else {
                    builder.idBuilder.setLength(0);
                    builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
                }
            }

            FunctionCall functionCall = toolCall.function();
            if (functionCall.name() != null) {
                builder.nameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
            }
            if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
                builder.argumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
            }
        }';

my $new = '        if (delta.toolCalls() != null && !delta.toolCalls().isEmpty()) {
            for (ToolCall toolCall : delta.toolCalls()) {
                int toolCallIndex = toolCall.index() != null ? toolCall.index() : fallbackToolCallIndex.get();

                ToolExecutionRequestBuilder builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
                        toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());

                // When index is null and a different tool call id appears, increment the fallback index
                if (toolCall.index() == null
                        && toolCall.id() != null
                        && !builder.idBuilder.isEmpty()
                        && !builder.idBuilder.toString().equals(toolCall.id())) {
                    toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.incrementAndGet();
                    builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
                            toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
                }

                if (toolCall.id() != null) {
                    if (accumulateToolCallId) {
                        builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
                    } else {
                        builder.idBuilder.setLength(0);
                        builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
                    }
                }

                FunctionCall functionCall = toolCall.function();
                if (functionCall.name() != null) {
                    builder.nameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
                }
                if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
                    builder.argumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
                }
            }
        }';

if (index($content, $old) != -1) {
    $content =~ s/\Q$old\E/$new/;
    open(my $out, '>', $file) or die "Cannot write $file: $!";
    print $out $content;
    close($out);
    print "Successfully replaced!\n";
} else {
    print "OLD string not found!\n";
    # Let's debug - find the toolCalls line
    my @lines = split("\n", $content);
    for my $i (0..$#lines) {
        if ($lines[$i] =~ /toolCalls/) {
            print "Line ".($i+1).": ".$lines[$i]."\n";
        }
    }
}
