     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.openai;
     2	
     3	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrBlank;
     4	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.Utils.isNullOrEmpty;
     5	import static dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.OpenAiUtils.finishReasonFrom;
     6	import static dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.OpenAiUtils.tokenUsageFrom;
     7	import static java.util.stream.Collectors.toList;
     8	
     9	import dev.langchain4j.Internal;
    10	import dev.langchain4j.agent.tool.ToolExecutionRequest;
    11	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
    12	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.SuccessfulHttpResponse;
    13	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.sse.ServerSentEvent;
    14	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
    15	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.ParsedAndRawResponse;
    16	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ChatCompletionChoice;
    17	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ChatCompletionResponse;
    18	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.Delta;
    19	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.FunctionCall;
    20	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.ToolCall;
    21	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.completion.CompletionChoice;
    22	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.completion.CompletionResponse;
    23	import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.shared.Usage;
    24	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.FinishReason;
    25	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
    26	import java.util.ArrayList;
    27	import java.util.List;
    28	import java.util.Map;
    29	import java.util.Queue;
    30	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    31	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentLinkedQueue;
    32	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicInteger;
    33	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
    34	
    35	/**
    36	 * This class needs to be thread safe because it is called when a streaming result comes back
    37	 * and there is no guarantee that this thread will be the same as the one that initiated the request,
    38	 * in fact it almost certainly won't be.
    39	 */
    40	@Internal
    41	public class OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder {
    42	
    43	    private final StringBuffer contentBuilder = new StringBuffer();
    44	    private final StringBuffer reasoningContentBuilder;
    45	
    46	    private final StringBuffer toolNameBuilder = new StringBuffer(); // legacy
    47	    private final StringBuffer toolArgumentsBuilder = new StringBuffer(); // legacy
    48	
    49	    private final Map<Integer, ToolExecutionRequestBuilder> indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder =
    50	            new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    51	    private final AtomicInteger fallbackToolCallIndex = new AtomicInteger(0);
    52	
    53	    private final AtomicReference<String> id = new AtomicReference<>();
    54	    private final AtomicReference<Long> created = new AtomicReference<>();
    55	    private final AtomicReference<String> model = new AtomicReference<>();
    56	    private final AtomicReference<String> serviceTier = new AtomicReference<>();
    57	    private final AtomicReference<String> systemFingerprint = new AtomicReference<>();
    58	    private final AtomicReference<TokenUsage> tokenUsage = new AtomicReference<>();
    59	    private final AtomicReference<FinishReason> finishReason = new AtomicReference<>();
    60	    private final AtomicReference<SuccessfulHttpResponse> rawHttpResponse = new AtomicReference<>();
    61	    private final Queue<ServerSentEvent> rawServerSentEvents = new ConcurrentLinkedQueue<>();
    62	
    63	    private final boolean returnThinking;
    64	    private final boolean accumulateToolCallId;
    65	
    66	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder() {
    67	        this(false, true);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean returnThinking) {
    71	        this(returnThinking, true);
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    public OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder(boolean returnThinking, boolean accumulateToolCallId) {
    75	        this.returnThinking = returnThinking;
    76	        this.accumulateToolCallId = accumulateToolCallId;
    77	        if (returnThinking) {
    78	            this.reasoningContentBuilder = new StringBuffer();
    79	        } else {
    80	            this.reasoningContentBuilder = null;
    81	        }
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    public void append(ParsedAndRawResponse<ChatCompletionResponse> parsedAndRawResponse) {
    85	        if (parsedAndRawResponse != null) {
    86	            if (parsedAndRawResponse.rawHttpResponse() != null) {
    87	                rawHttpResponse.set(parsedAndRawResponse.rawHttpResponse());
    88	            }
    89	            if (parsedAndRawResponse.rawServerSentEvent() != null) {
    90	                rawServerSentEvents.add(parsedAndRawResponse.rawServerSentEvent());
    91	            }
    92	
    93	            append(parsedAndRawResponse.parsedResponse());
    94	        }
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    public void append(ChatCompletionResponse partialResponse) {
    98	        if (partialResponse == null) {
    99	            return;
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.id())) {
   103	            this.id.set(partialResponse.id());
   104	        }
   105	        if (partialResponse.created() != null) {
   106	            this.created.set(partialResponse.created());
   107	        }
   108	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.model())) {
   109	            this.model.set(partialResponse.model());
   110	        }
   111	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.serviceTier())) {
   112	            this.serviceTier.set(partialResponse.serviceTier());
   113	        }
   114	        if (!isNullOrBlank(partialResponse.systemFingerprint())) {
   115	            this.systemFingerprint.set(partialResponse.systemFingerprint());
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        Usage usage = partialResponse.usage();
   119	        if (usage != null) {
   120	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsageFrom(usage));
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        List<ChatCompletionChoice> choices = partialResponse.choices();
   124	        if (isNullOrEmpty(choices)) {
   125	            return;
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        ChatCompletionChoice chatCompletionChoice = choices.get(0);
   129	        if (chatCompletionChoice == null) {
   130	            return;
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        String finishReason = chatCompletionChoice.finishReason();
   134	        if (finishReason != null) {
   135	            this.finishReason.set(finishReasonFrom(finishReason));
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        Delta delta = chatCompletionChoice.delta();
   139	        if (delta == null) {
   140	            return;
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        String content = delta.content();
   144	        if (!isNullOrEmpty(content)) {
   145	            this.contentBuilder.append(content);
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        String reasoningContent = delta.reasoningContent();
   149	        if (returnThinking && !isNullOrEmpty(reasoningContent)) {
   150	            this.reasoningContentBuilder.append(reasoningContent);
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        if (delta.functionCall() != null) {
   154	            FunctionCall functionCall = delta.functionCall();
   155	
   156	            if (functionCall.name() != null) {
   157	                this.toolNameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
   158	            }
   159	
   160	            if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
   161	                this.toolArgumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
   162	            }
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        if (delta.toolCalls() != null && !delta.toolCalls().isEmpty()) {
   166	            for (ToolCall toolCall : delta.toolCalls()) {
   167	                int toolCallIndex = toolCall.index() != null ? toolCall.index() : fallbackToolCallIndex.get();
   168	
   169	                ToolExecutionRequestBuilder builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
   170	                        toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
   171	
   172	                // When index is null and a different tool call id appears, increment the fallback index
   173	                if (toolCall.index() == null
   174	                        && toolCall.id() != null
   175	                        && !builder.idBuilder.isEmpty()
   176	                        && !builder.idBuilder.toString().equals(toolCall.id())) {
   177	                    toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.incrementAndGet();
   178	                    builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
   179	                            toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
   180	                }
   181	
   182	                if (toolCall.id() != null) {
   183	                    if (accumulateToolCallId) {
   184	                        builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
   185	                    } else {
   186	                        builder.idBuilder.setLength(0);
   187	                        builder.idBuilder.append(toolCall.id());
   188	                    }
   189	                }
   190	
   191	                FunctionCall functionCall = toolCall.function();
   192	                if (functionCall.name() != null) {
   193	                    builder.nameBuilder.append(functionCall.name());
   194	                }
   195	                if (functionCall.arguments() != null) {
   196	                    builder.argumentsBuilder.append(functionCall.arguments());
   197	                }
   198	            }
   199	        }
   200	    }
   201	
   202	    public void append(CompletionResponse partialResponse) {
   203	        if (partialResponse == null) {
   204	            return;
   205	        }
   206	
   207	        Usage usage = partialResponse.usage();
   208	        if (usage != null) {
   209	            this.tokenUsage.set(tokenUsageFrom(usage));
   210	        }
   211	
   212	        List<CompletionChoice> choices = partialResponse.choices();
   213	        if (isNullOrEmpty(choices)) {
   214	            return;
   215	        }
   216	
   217	        CompletionChoice completionChoice = choices.get(0);
   218	        if (completionChoice == null) {
   219	            return;
   220	        }
   221	
   222	        String finishReason = completionChoice.finishReason();
   223	        if (finishReason != null) {
   224	            this.finishReason.set(finishReasonFrom(finishReason));
   225	        }
   226	
   227	        String token = completionChoice.text();
   228	        if (token != null) {
   229	            this.contentBuilder.append(token);
   230	        }
   231	    }
   232	
   233	    public ChatResponse build() {
   234	        return ChatResponse.builder()
   235	                .aiMessage(buildAiMessage())
   236	                .metadata(buildMetadata())
   237	                .build();
   238	    }
   239	
   240	    private AiMessage buildAiMessage() {
   241	        String text = contentBuilder.toString();
   242	
   243	        String thinking = null;
   244	        if (returnThinking) {
   245	            thinking = reasoningContentBuilder.toString();
   246	        }
   247	
   248	        return AiMessage.builder()
   249	                .text(isNullOrEmpty(text) ? null : text)
   250	                .thinking(isNullOrEmpty(thinking) ? null : thinking)
   251	                .toolExecutionRequests(buildToolExecutionRequests())
   252	                .build();
   253	    }
   254	
   255	    private List<ToolExecutionRequest> buildToolExecutionRequests() {
   256	        List<ToolExecutionRequest> toolExecutionRequests = new ArrayList<>();
   257	
   258	        // legacy
   259	        String toolName = toolNameBuilder.toString();
   260	        if (!toolName.isEmpty()) {
   261	            ToolExecutionRequest toolExecutionRequest = ToolExecutionRequest.builder()
   262	                    .name(toolName)
   263	                    .arguments(toolArgumentsBuilder.toString())
   264	                    .build();
   265	            toolExecutionRequests.add(toolExecutionRequest);
   266	        }
   267	
   268	        if (!indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.isEmpty()) {
   269	            List<ToolExecutionRequest> toolRequests = indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.values().stream()
   270	                    .map(it -> ToolExecutionRequest.builder()
   271	                            .id(it.idBuilder.toString())
   272	                            .name(it.nameBuilder.toString())
   273	                            .arguments(it.argumentsBuilder.toString())
   274	                            .build())
   275	                    .collect(toList());
   276	            toolExecutionRequests.addAll(toolRequests);
   277	        }
   278	
   279	        return toolExecutionRequests;
   280	    }
   281	
   282	    private OpenAiChatResponseMetadata buildMetadata() {
   283	        return OpenAiChatResponseMetadata.builder()
   284	                .id(id.get())
   285	                .modelName(model.get())
   286	                .tokenUsage(tokenUsage.get())
   287	                .finishReason(finishReason.get())
   288	                .created(created.get())
   289	                .serviceTier(serviceTier.get())
   290	                .systemFingerprint(systemFingerprint.get())
   291	                .rawHttpResponse(rawHttpResponse.get())
   292	                .rawServerSentEvents(new ArrayList<>(rawServerSentEvents))
   293	                .build();
   294	    }
   295	
   296	    private static class ToolExecutionRequestBuilder {
   297	
   298	        private final StringBuffer idBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   299	        private final StringBuffer nameBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   300	        private final StringBuffer argumentsBuilder = new StringBuffer();
   301	    }
   302	}

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/TestFix.java << 'EOF'
package dev.langchain4j.model.openai;

import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;

import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;
import dev.langchain4j.model.openai.internal.chat.*;
import java.util.List;

public class TestFix {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        // Test 1: Multiple tool calls in single delta with indexes
        OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder builder = new OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder();

        ToolCall tc1 = ToolCall.builder()
                .id("call_1")
                .index(0)
                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
                .function(FunctionCall.builder().name("run_sql").arguments("{\"q\":\"SELECT 1\"}").build())
                .build();

        ToolCall tc2 = ToolCall.builder()
                .id("call_2")
                .index(1)
                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
                .function(FunctionCall.builder().name("run_sql").arguments("{\"q\":\"SELECT 2\"}").build())
                .build();

        ChatCompletionResponse partial = ChatCompletionResponse.builder()
                .id("resp_1")
                .model("openai-compatible-model")
                .choices(List.of(ChatCompletionChoice.builder()
                        .index(0)
                        .delta(Delta.builder().toolCalls(List.of(tc1, tc2)).build())
                        .build()))
                .build();

        builder.append(partial);
        ChatResponse response = builder.build();

        System.out.println("Test 1 - Multiple tool calls with indexes in single delta:");
        System.out.println("  Tool execution requests size: " + response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size());
        System.out.println("  Expected: 2");
        
        if (response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size() == 2) {
            System.out.println("  PASS");
        } else {
            System.out.println("  FAIL: Expected 2 but got " + response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size());
            System.exit(1);
        }
        
        // Test 2: Multiple tool calls with null indexes (Gemini style)
        OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder builder2 = new OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder();
        
        ToolCall tc3 = ToolCall.builder()
                .id("call_a")
                .index(null)
                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
                .function(FunctionCall.builder().name("tool_a").arguments("{}").build())
                .build();
        
        ToolCall tc4 = ToolCall.builder()
                .id("call_b")
                .index(null)
                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
                .function(FunctionCall.builder().name("tool_b").arguments("{}").build())
                .build();
        
        ChatCompletionResponse partial2 = ChatCompletionResponse.builder()
                .id("resp_2")
                .model("gemini")
                .choices(List.of(ChatCompletionChoice.builder()
                        .index(0)
                        .delta(Delta.builder().toolCalls(List.of(tc3, tc4)).build())
                        .build()))
                .build();
        
        builder2.append(partial2);
        ChatResponse response2 = builder2.build();
        
        System.out.println("Test 2 - Multiple tool calls with null indexes in single delta:");
        System.out.println("  Tool execution requests size: " + response2.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size());
        System.out.println("  Expected: 2");
        
        if (response2.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size() == 2) {
            System.out.println("  PASS");
        } else {
            System.out.println("  FAIL: Expected 2 but got " + response2.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size());
            System.exit(1);
        }
        
        System.out.println("All tests passed!");
    }
}

import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.response.ChatResponse;

import java.util.List;

        ToolCall tc2 = ToolCall.builder()
                .id("call_2")
                .index(1)

        ChatCompletionResponse partial = ChatCompletionResponse.builder()

                .choices(List.of(ChatCompletionChoice.builder()
                        .index(0)
                        .delta(Delta.builder().toolCalls(List.of(tc1, tc2)).build())
                        .build()))
                .build();

        builder.append(partial);

        System.out.println("Test 1 - Multiple tool calls with indexes in single delta:");
        System.out.println("  Tool execution requests size: " + response.aiMessage().toolExecutionRequests().size());
        System.out.println("  Expected: 2");

        System.out.println("  " + (pass1 ? "PASS" : "FAIL"));
        
        // Test 2: Multiple tool calls with null indexes

                .id("call_a")

                .type(ToolType.FUNCTION)
                .function(FunctionCall.builder().name("tool_b").arguments("{}").build())
                .build();

        System.out.println("  Expected: 2");

        System.out.println("  " + (pass2 ? "PASS" : "FAIL"));

        }
    }


So the `handle` method already handles this correctly. The only bug was in `OpenAiStreamingResponseBuilder.append()`.

Now let me think about edge cases:

1. **Single tool call in delta** - Should still work fine. The for loop will just iterate once.
2. **Multiple tool calls in single delta with indexes** - This is the main fix scenario. Now all tool calls will be processed.
3. **Multiple tool calls in single delta with null indexes** - The fallback logic should handle this. The first null-index tool call gets `fallbackToolCallIndex.get()` (which is 0). The second null-index tool call: since `builder.idBuilder` is empty (we just created it for index 0), but wait - let me trace through this more carefully.

For null indexes, the code does:
```java
int toolCallIndex = toolCall.index() != null ? toolCall.index() : fallbackToolCallIndex.get();
// fallbackToolCallIndex starts at 0, so toolCallIndex = 0 for the first one

ToolExecutionRequestBuilder builder = this.indexToToolExecutionRequestBuilder.computeIfAbsent(
        toolCallIndex, idx -> new ToolExecutionRequestBuilder());
// Creates a new builder for index 0

// Then checks if index is null and a different tool call id appears (not first time)
if (toolCall.index() == null
        && toolCall.id() != null
        && !builder.idBuilder.isEmpty()
        && !builder.idBuilder.toString().equals(toolCall.id())) {
    ...
}
```

For the first tool call (tc3, id="call_a"), `builder.idBuilder` is empty, so the condition fails (good - we use the builder for index 0).

For the second tool call (tc4, id="call_b"), `toolCall.index()` is null, so `toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.get()` which is still 0 (hasn't been incremented). Then `computeIfAbsent` returns the existing builder for index 0. Now `builder.idBuilder` is not empty (it has "call_a"), and it doesn't equal "call_b", so the condition is true. It increments fallbackToolCallIndex to 1, and creates a new builder for index 1. 

So this should work correctly for null indexes as well.

But wait - there's a subtle issue with the null-index case when multiple tool calls come in the same delta. Let me trace again:

For the first null-index tool call (id="call_a"):
- `toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.get()` = 0
- `computeIfAbsent(0)` creates new builder (idBuilder empty)
- Check: `toolCall.index() == null` (true), `toolCall.id() != null` ("call_a"), `!builder.idBuilder.isEmpty()` (false - empty) → condition fails, no increment
- Then we append "call_a" to builder.idBuilder

For the second null-index tool call (id="call_b"):
- `toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.get()` = 0 (still 0, hasn't been incremented)
- `computeIfAbsent(0)` returns existing builder (idBuilder = "call_a")
- Check: `toolCall.index() == null` (true), `toolCall.id() != null` ("call_b"), `!builder.idBuilder.isEmpty()` (true), `!builder.idBuilder.toString().equals(toolCall.id())` → "call_a" != "call_b" → true
- So: `toolCallIndex = fallbackToolCallIndex.incrementAndGet()` = 1, creates new builder for index 1
- Then we append "call_b" to the new builder's idBuilder

This is correct! Both tool calls get their own builders.
